		GROUP BY d.codmedico),( ISNULL(SUM(c.cantidad * c.precunit - c.Descuento),0)  + 
		ISNULL((SELECT  SUM(l.cantidad * l.precunit - l.Descuento) total_laser From VIEW_Ventas_Medicos_Laser l 
    	WHERE  (fechafac BETWEEN '06-25-2018' and '06-25-2018') AND (l.statfact <> '2') AND (l.Prod_serv = 'M') and l.codmedico =c.codmedico and   l.codmedico in('004','315','317','319','320','327','328','329','330','331') 
    	GROUP BY l.codmedico ),0)  + 
		ISNULL((SELECT  SUM(b.cantidad * b.precunit - b.Descuento) total_suero  From VIEW_Ventas_Medicos_Suero b 
    	WHERE  (fechafac BETWEEN '06-25-2018' and '06-25-2018') AND (b.statfact <> '2') AND (b.Prod_serv = 'S') and b.codmedico = c.codmedico  and b.codmedico in('004','315','317','319','320','327','328','329','330','331') 
    	GROUP BY b.codmedico ),0)  ) ) total_ventas 
		From VIEW_Ventas_Medicos c 
    	WHERE  (fechafac BETWEEN '06-25-2018' and '06-25-2018') AND (c.statfact <> '2') AND (c.Prod_serv = 'P') and c.codmedico in('004','315','317','319','320','327','328','329','330','331') 
    	GROUP BY c.codmedico
